CPU-specific code. The core mechanism uses a dispatch table to route bytecode execution.\\n\\n**Architecture Overview:**\\n\\nThe interpreter dispatch mechanism consists of three main components:\\n\\n1. **Dispatch Table System** (src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreter.hpp/cpp):\\n   - Defines the `DispatchTable` class which maintains three tables: `_active_table` (current), `_normal_table` (normal mode), and `_safept_table` (safepoint mode)\\n   - Each table maps 256 bytecode values to entry points across 10 TosState (Top-Of-Stack Cache states)\\n   - The `dispatch_table()` method returns pointers to these dispatch tables\\n   - Static instances `_active_table`, `_normal_table`, and `_safept_table` maintain the actual dispatch entries\\n\\n2. **Template Generation** (src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreterGenerator.cpp):\\n   - `generate_all()` creates code templates for each bytecode instruction\\n   - `set_entry_points_for_all_bytes()` populates the dispatch tables with generated code addresses\\n   - `set_safepoints_for_all_bytes()` creates safe entry points for garbage collection\\n   - Each bytecode has up to 10 entry points (one per TosState) for performance optimization\\n\\n3. **Template Definition** (src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateTable.hpp/cpp):\\n   - `Template` class describes code generation properties for each bytecode\\n   - `TemplateTable` maintains static template definitions for all bytecodes\\n   - Each template has flags (uses_bcp, does_dispatch, calls_vm, is_wide) and generator functions\\n\\n**CPU-Specific Dispatch Implementation:**\\n\\nEach CPU architecture implements dispatch via InterpreterMacroAssembler classes:\\n\\n- **X86** (src/hotspot/cpu/x86/interp_masm_x86.cpp): dispatch_next(), dispatch_via(), dispatch_base() - uses indirect jumps through dispatch table with bytecode as index\\n- **ARM64** (src/hotspot/cpu/aarch64/interp_masm_aarch64.cpp): Similar dispatch mechanism with ARM64-specific addressing\\n- **PowerPC** (src/hotspot/cpu/ppc/interp_masm_ppc_64.cpp): Uses PPC load and count register instructions for dispatch\\n- **S390** (src/hotspot/cpu/s390/interp_masm_s390.cpp): S390-specific dispatch implementation\\n- **RISC-V** (src/hotspot/cpu/riscv/interp_masm_riscv.cpp): RISC-V dispatch with register-indirect jumps\\n- **ARM** (src/hotspot/cpu/arm/interp_masm_arm.cpp): 32-bit ARM dispatch mechanism\\n\\nThe dispatch flow:\\n1. Load next bytecode from code buffer (bcp)\\n2. Use bytecode as index into dispatch table\\n3. Jump to table entry (interpreter code for that bytecode)\\n4. Bytecode handler executes and loads next bytecode\\n5. Dispatch repeats\\n\\n**Method Entry Points:**\\n\\nTemplateInterpreterGenerator variants generate method entry points:\\n- `generate_method_entry()` creates entry code for different method types (native, synchronized, etc.)\\n- `generate_normal_entry()` sets up interpreter frame and initializes entry points\\n- `generate_native_entry()` for native methods\\n- Return entry points via `generate_return_entry_for()` for each TosState\\n\\n**Zero Interpreter Alternative:**\\n\\nFor architectures without JIT compilation:\\n- src/hotspot/share/interpreter/zero/bytecodeInterpreter.cpp implements a switch-based interpreter loop\\n- Direct interpretation without templates\\n- Used on platforms like MIPS, S390 without JIT support\\n\\n**Key Files by Function:**\\n\\n- **Dispatch table initialization**: templateInterpreter.cpp (static instances and copying)\\n- **Entry point setup**: templateInterpreterGenerator.cpp (generic) + per-arch files (CPU-specific generation)\\n- **Bytecode handlers**: templateTable*.cpp files (one per architecture)\\n- **Assembly macros**: interp_masm_*.cpp files for dispatch instructions\\n- **Runtime support**: interpreterRT_*.cpp for calling runtime functions from interpreter\\n- **Frame setup**: abstractInterpreter_*.cpp for frame layout calculations\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":857,"cache_read_input_tokens":96736,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":857},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a1cf1d10-5ba3-4264-a731-7ee6f928131f","uuid":"eb23d2b8-e6f5-4ab9-8558-6075b22998b4"}

\"symbol\": \"generate\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The JVM bytecode interpreter main dispatch loop in OpenJDK is implemented through a template-based architecture distributed across shared and CPU-specific code. The core mechanism uses a dispatch table to route bytecode execution.\\n\\n**Architecture Overview:**\\n\\nThe interpreter dispatch mechanism consists of three main components:\\n\\n1. **Dispatch Table System** (src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreter.hpp/cpp):\\n   - Defines the `DispatchTable` class which maintains three tables: `_active_table` (current), `_normal_table` (normal mode), and `_safept_table` (safepoint mode)\\n   - Each table maps 256 bytecode values to entry points across 10 TosState (Top-Of-Stack Cache states)\\n   - The `dispatch_table()` method returns pointers to these dispatch tables\\n   - Static instances `_active_table`, `_normal_table`, and `_safept_table` maintain the actual dispatch entries\\n\\n2. **Template Generation** (src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateInterpreterGenerator.cpp):\\n   - `generate_all()` creates code templates for each bytecode instruction\\n   - `set_entry_points_for_all_bytes()` populates the dispatch tables with generated code addresses\\n   - `set_safepoints_for_all_bytes()` creates safe entry points for garbage collection\\n   - Each bytecode has up to 10 entry points (one per TosState) for performance optimization\\n\\n3. **Template Definition** (src/hotspot/share/interpreter/templateTable.hpp/cpp):\\n   - `Template` class describes code generation properties for each bytecode\\n   - `TemplateTable` maintains static template definitions for all bytecodes\\n   - Each template has flags (uses_bcp, does_dispatch, calls_vm, is_wide) and generator functions\\n\\n**CPU-Specific Dispatch Implementation:**\\n\\nEach CPU architecture implements dispatch via InterpreterMacroAssembler classes:\\n\\n- **X86** (src/hotspot/cpu/x86/interp_masm_x86.cpp): dispatch_next(), dispatch_via(), dispatch_base() - uses indirect jumps through dispatch table with bytecode as index\\n- **ARM64** (src/hotspot/cpu/aarch64/interp_masm_aarch64.cpp): Similar dispatch mechanism with ARM64-specific addressing\\n- **PowerPC** (src/hotspot/cpu/ppc/interp_masm_ppc_64.cpp): Uses PPC load and count register instructions for dispatch\\n- **S390** (src/hotspot/cpu/s390/interp_masm_s390.cpp): S390-specific dispatch implementation\\n- **RISC-V** (src/hotspot/cpu/riscv/interp_masm_riscv.cpp): RISC-V dispatch with register-indirect jumps\\n- **ARM** (src/hotspot/cpu/arm/interp_masm_arm.cpp): 32-bit ARM dispatch mechanism\\n\\nThe dispatch flow:\\n1. Load next bytecode from code buffer (bcp)\\n2. Use bytecode as index into dispatch table\\n3. Jump to table entry (interpreter code for that bytecode)\\n4. Bytecode handler executes and loads next bytecode\\n5. Dispatch repeats\\n\\n**Method Entry Points:**\\n\\nTemplateInterpreterGenerator variants generate method entry points:\\n- `generate_method_entry()` creates entry code for different method types (native, synchronized, etc.)\\n- `generate_normal_entry()` sets up interpreter frame and initializes entry points\\n- `generate_native_entry()` for native methods\\n- Return entry points via `generate_return_entry_for()` for each TosState\\n\\n**Zero Interpreter Alternative:**\\n\\nFor architectures without JIT compilation:\\n- src/hotspot/share/interpreter/zero/bytecodeInterpreter.cpp implements a switch-based interpreter loop\\n- Direct interpretation without templates\\n- Used on platforms like MIPS, S390 without JIT support\\n\\n**Key Files by Function:**\\n\\n- **Dispatch table initialization**: templateInterpreter.cpp (static instances and copying)\\n- **Entry point setup**: templateInterpreterGenerator.cpp (generic) + per-arch files (CPU-specific generation)\\n- **Bytecode handlers**: templateTable*.cpp files (one per architecture)\\n- **Assembly macros**: interp_masm_*.cpp files for dispatch instructions\\n- **Runtime support**: interpreterRT_*.cpp for calling runtime functions from interpreter\\n- **Frame setup**: abstractInterpreter_*.cpp for frame layout calculations\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
